+import Foundation
+import Testing
+
+/// Architecture regression tests for AppState.
+///
+/// Locks post-Phase-F (#501) state so AppState does not silently re-accrete
+/// toward a god-object. Tests parse the source file directly rather than
+/// constructing an AppState instance — AppState's init pulls in real audio
+/// capture, ASR, pipelines, and Tasks that should not run inside a unit test.
+///
+/// Ceilings are documented in `.claude/rules/architecture-rules.md` under
+/// `Architectural Ceilings`. Raising a ceiling requires a Bible changelog entry.
+@Suite struct AppStateCeilingsTests {
+
+  /// Concrete-collaborator count ceiling. Locked at post-Phase-F baseline = 19.
+  /// Counts top-level `let` declarations on AppState whose type is non-primitive.
+  /// Existentials (`any X`) count as collaborators.
+  @Test func appStateConcreteCollaboratorCeilingHolds() throws {
+    let body = try classBodyOfAppState()
+    let count = countTopLevelLetCollaborators(in: body)
+    #expect(
+      count <= 19,
+      """
+      AppState concrete-collaborator ceiling exceeded: \(count) > 19. \
+      See .claude/rules/architecture-rules.md `Architectural Ceilings`.
+      """)
+  }
+
+  /// File line-count ceiling. Locked at post-Phase-F (954) + ~10% rounded to 1050.
+  /// Soft backstop against scope creep.
+  @Test func appStateLineCountCeilingHolds() throws {
+    let url = appStateURL()
+    let source = try String(contentsOf: url, encoding: .utf8)
+    let lineCount = source.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false).count
+    #expect(
+      lineCount <= 1050,
+      """
+      AppState line count exceeded: \(lineCount) > 1050. \
+      See .claude/rules/architecture-rules.md `Architectural Ceilings`.
+      """)
+  }
+}
+
+private func appStateURL() -> URL {
+  // SPM tests run with cwd = package root.
+  URL(fileURLWithPath: "Sources/EnviousWispr/App/AppState.swift")
+}
+
+private func classBodyOfAppState() throws -> String {
+  let source = try String(contentsOf: appStateURL(), encoding: .utf8)
+  guard let openRange = source.range(of: "final class AppState {") else {
+    Issue.record("AppState declaration not found at expected path/shape")
+    throw POSIXError(.ENOENT)
+  }
+  let openIdx = source.index(before: openRange.upperBound)  // points at '{'
+  var depth = 0
+  var idx = openIdx
+  while idx < source.endIndex {
+    let c = source[idx]
+    if c == "{" { depth += 1 }
+    if c == "}" {
+      depth -= 1
+      if depth == 0 { return String(source[source.index(after: openIdx)..<idx]) }
+    }
+    idx = source.index(after: idx)
+  }
+  Issue.record("AppState class body has unbalanced braces")
+  throw POSIXError(.EILSEQ)
+}
+
+private func countTopLevelLetCollaborators(in body: String) -> Int {
+  // Top-level = brace-depth 0 within the class body.
+  // Match `let <ident>` declarations preceded by any combination of:
+  //   - Swift attributes (e.g. `@ObservationIgnored`, `@Published`)
+  //   - One access modifier (public/internal/private/fileprivate/package/open)
+  // Skip primitives (Bool/Int/String/closures/Tasks).
+  var depth = 0
+  var collaborators = 0
+  for line in body.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false) {
+    let opens = line.filter { $0 == "{" }.count
+    let closes = line.filter { $0 == "}" }.count
+    let depthForThisLine = depth - max(0, closes - opens)
+    if depthForThisLine == 0 {
+      let s = String(line)
+      if isCollaboratorLetDeclaration(s) && !isPrimitiveTyped(s) {
+        collaborators += 1
+      }
+    }
+    depth += opens - closes
+  }
+  return collaborators
+}
+
+private let collaboratorLetPattern: String = {
+  let attrs = #"(@[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*[[:space:]]+)*"#
+  let access = #"(public|internal|private|fileprivate|package|open)?"#
+  return "^[[:space:]]*\(attrs)\(access)[[:space:]]*let[[:space:]]+[A-Za-z_]"
+}()
+
+private func isCollaboratorLetDeclaration(_ line: String) -> Bool {
+  return line.range(of: collaboratorLetPattern, options: .regularExpression) != nil
+}
+
+private func isPrimitiveTyped(_ line: String) -> Bool {
+  // Architectural collaborators are concrete app/library types and protocol
+  // existentials. Plain values are not collaborators.
+  let primitives = [
+    ": Bool", ": Int", ": String", ": Double", ": Float",
+    "Task<", ": ((", "= false", "= true",
+  ]
+  return primitives.contains { line.contains($0) }
+}

+import Foundation
+import Testing
+
+/// Audit meta-rec #1 (Bible §11): confessional `public` exposure across module
+/// boundaries is a known architecture smell. This test fails if a `public`
+/// declaration in any non-executable module has a confessional `TODO` comment
+/// within ±3 lines.
+///
+/// Pattern requires both `TODO` AND a structural-cross-module keyword in the
+/// surrounding window. The conjunction avoids false positives like
+/// `phaseString` (function name), `narrow_margin` (telemetry field), and
+/// "single-phase" (literal phase counting in algorithms) that have no
+/// architectural meaning.
+@Suite struct CrossModulePublicGuardTests {
+
+  @Test func noConfessionalCrossModulePublicExists() throws {
+    let sourcesRoot = URL(fileURLWithPath: "Sources")
+    var offenders: [String] = []
+
+    // Exclude executable targets (app shell + XPC services). These are not
+    // libraries that other modules consume, so cross-module-public is not a
+    // meaningful concept for them.
+    let executableTargets: Set<String> = [
+      "EnviousWispr",
+      "EnviousWisprAudioService",
+      "EnviousWisprASRService",
+    ]
+
+    let modules = try FileManager.default.contentsOfDirectory(
+      at: sourcesRoot, includingPropertiesForKeys: nil
+    )
+    .filter { (try? $0.resourceValues(forKeys: [.isDirectoryKey]).isDirectory) == true }
+    .filter { !executableTargets.contains($0.lastPathComponent) }
+
+    for module in modules {
+      let files = try filesRecursively(at: module).filter { $0.pathExtension == "swift" }
+      for file in files {
+        let source = try String(contentsOf: file, encoding: .utf8)
+        let lines = source.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false)
+          .map(String.init)
+        for (idx, line) in lines.enumerated() where line.contains("public ") {
+          let lo = max(0, idx - 3)
+          let hi = min(lines.count - 1, idx + 3)
+          let window = lines[lo...hi].joined(separator: " ").lowercased()
+          let hasTodo = window.contains("todo")
+          let hasStructural =
+            window.contains("narrow")
+            || window.contains("temporary")
+            || window.contains("cross-module") || window.contains("cross module")
+            || window.range(of: #"phase\s*[a-z\d]+"#, options: .regularExpression) != nil
+          if hasTodo && hasStructural {
+            offenders.append(
+              "\(file.path):\(idx + 1): \(line.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces))")
+          }
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    #expect(
+      offenders.isEmpty,
+      """
+      Confessional cross-module `public` found (TODO + structural keyword within ±3 lines):
+      \(offenders.joined(separator: "\n"))
+      """)
+  }
+}
+
+private func filesRecursively(at dir: URL) throws -> [URL] {
+  guard
+    let enumerator = FileManager.default.enumerator(
+      at: dir, includingPropertiesForKeys: [.isRegularFileKey])
+  else { return [] }
+  return enumerator.compactMap { $0 as? URL }
+    .filter { (try? $0.resourceValues(forKeys: [.isRegularFileKey]).isRegularFile) == true }
+}

+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+# Validates SPM target dependency direction by grepping `import` statements per module.
+# Fails on backward edges. Run from package root.
+#
+# Authoritative dep graph (verified against Package.swift on 2026-04-30).
+# Edit `permitted_imports_for` below when Package.swift changes (and update the
+# Bible if the new edge represents an architectural decision):
+#   EnviousWispr           -> Core, Storage, PostProcessing, Audio, Services, ASR, LLM, Pipeline (executable, top of stack)
+#   EnviousWisprAudioService -> Core, Audio (XPC executable)
+#   EnviousWisprASRService -> Core, ASR, Audio (XPC executable)
+#   EnviousWisprPipeline   -> Core, ASR, Audio, LLM, PostProcessing, Services, Storage
+#   EnviousWisprASR        -> Core, Audio
+#   EnviousWisprServices   -> Core
+#   EnviousWisprLLM        -> Core
+#   EnviousWisprAudio      -> Core
+#   EnviousWisprPostProcessing -> Core
+#   EnviousWisprStorage    -> Core
+#   EnviousWisprCore       -> (no app deps)
+#
+# Bash-3.2 compatible (macOS system /bin/bash). No associative arrays.
+
+set -euo pipefail
+
+# Returns the space-separated list of allowed EnviousWispr* deps for a target,
+# echoing nothing for "no deps allowed", and returning non-zero for unknown.
+permitted_imports_for() {
+  case "$1" in
+    EnviousWisprCore)              echo "" ;;
+    EnviousWisprAudio)             echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
+    EnviousWisprASR)               echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprAudio" ;;
+    EnviousWisprPostProcessing)    echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
+    EnviousWisprStorage)           echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
+    EnviousWisprLLM)               echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
+    EnviousWisprServices)          echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
+    EnviousWisprPipeline)          echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprASR EnviousWisprAudio EnviousWisprLLM EnviousWisprPostProcessing EnviousWisprServices EnviousWisprStorage" ;;
+    EnviousWisprAudioService)      echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprAudio" ;;
+    EnviousWisprASRService)        echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprASR EnviousWisprAudio" ;;
+    EnviousWispr)                  echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprStorage EnviousWisprPostProcessing EnviousWisprAudio EnviousWisprServices EnviousWisprASR EnviousWisprLLM EnviousWisprPipeline" ;;
+    *)                             return 1 ;;
+  esac
+}
+
+violations=0
+modules_scanned=0
+
+# Match `import EnviousWispr...` with:
+#   - Optional Swift attributes (e.g. `@preconcurrency`, `@_implementationOnly`,
+#     `@_spi(Internal)` — parenthesized argument allowed)
+#   - Optional leading whitespace
+#   - Optional import-kind tokens (`struct`, `class`, `enum`, `protocol`, `func`,
+#     `var`, `let`, `typealias`) for scoped imports like
+#     `import struct EnviousWisprPipeline.Foo`
+# Requires start-of-line anchoring to avoid matching literal text inside
+# comments or strings.
+import_kinds='(typealias|struct|class|enum|protocol|let|var|func)'
+import_attr='(@[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*(\([^)]*\))?[[:space:]]+)*'
+import_grep_pattern="^[[:space:]]*${import_attr}import[[:space:]]+(${import_kinds}[[:space:]]+)?EnviousWispr"
+
+for module_dir in Sources/*/; do
+  module=$(basename "$module_dir")
+  if ! permitted=$(permitted_imports_for "$module"); then
+    echo "DEP-DIRECTION: unknown target '$module' under Sources/ — add to permitted_imports_for() or remove" >&2
+    violations=$((violations + 1))
+    continue
+  fi
+  modules_scanned=$((modules_scanned + 1))
+  while IFS= read -r line; do
+    file=$(echo "$line" | cut -d: -f1)
+    # Strip the leading `path:lineno:` prefix from grep + any line/block comment
+    # tail before extracting the module. Stripping comments matters because an
+    # inline `// EnviousWisprCore` after a forbidden `import EnviousWisprPipeline`
+    # would otherwise be picked up by the greedy sed below.
+    code=$(echo "$line" | cut -d: -f3- | sed -E 's|//.*$||; s|/\*.*$||')
+    # Extract the imported module name. Handles plain (`import EnviousWisprX`)
+    # and scoped (`import struct EnviousWisprX.Foo`) forms by anchoring the
+    # capture to the first `EnviousWispr<rest>` token AFTER the `import` keyword.
+    # `${import_kinds}` already wraps the alternation in `(...)`, so the outer
+    # `(${import_kinds}[[:space:]]+)?` is group 1 and the inner alternation is
+    # group 2. The EnviousWispr capture is group 3.
+    imp=$(echo "$code" | sed -E "s/^.*import[[:space:]]+(${import_kinds}[[:space:]]+)?(EnviousWispr[A-Za-z_]*).*/\\3/")
+    case "$imp" in
+      EnviousWispr*)
+        if ! echo " $permitted " | grep -q " $imp "; then
+          echo "DEP-DIRECTION: $file: '$module' imports '$imp' (not in allowed: $permitted)"
+          violations=$((violations + 1))
+        fi
+        ;;
+    esac
+  done < <(grep -rEn "$import_grep_pattern" "$module_dir" || true)
+done
+
+if [ "$violations" -gt 0 ]; then
+  echo "FAIL: $violations dep-direction violation(s)" >&2
+  exit 1
+fi
+echo "OK: dep-direction clean across $modules_scanned modules"

from pathlib import Path
body = Path('Sources/EnviousWispr/App/AppState.swift').read_text()

# rough find matching
s=body[start:]
d=1
end=start
for i,c in enumerate(body[start:], start):
    if c=='{': d+=1
    elif c=='}':
        d-=1
        if d==0:
            end=i; break
body=body[start:end]
import re
pat=re.compile(r'"'^['"\\s]*(?:@[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*[[:space:]]+)*(?:public|internal|private|fileprivate|package|open)?[[:space:]]*let[[:space:]]+[A-Za-z_]'.replace('[[:space:]]','\\\\s'))

d=0; cnt=0
for no,line in enumerate(body.split('\\n'),1):
    opens=line.count('{'); closes=line.count('}')
    depthFor=d-max(0,closes-opens)
    if depthFor==0 and pat.search(line) and not any(p in line for p in prims):
        print(no,line)
        cnt+=1
    d+=opens-closes
print('cnt',cnt, 'final depth', d)

+**Sign-Off: PROCEED-WITH-REVISIONS**
+
+The core AppState ceiling idea is sound, but the plan is not baseline-clean as written. The AppState numbers are correct; the cross-module TODO guard and dependency-direction script are the parts that need revision before implementation.
+
+AppState collaborator count: confirmed 19 under the Phase E definition: top-level `let`, non-primitive, including existentials. The list is: `permissions` [AppState.swift:18], `audioCapture` :19, `asrManager` :20, `keychainManager` :21, `hotkeyService` :22, `benchmark` :23, `recordingOverlay` :24, `setup` :29, `audioDeviceList` :30, `captureTelemetry` :31, `pipeline` :38, `whisperKitPipeline` :39, `polishService` :86, `settingsSync` :89, `transcriptCoordinator` :95, `customWordsCoordinator` :111, `customWordsPropagator` :118, `llmDiscovery` :121, `aiAvailability` :124. I agree with counting the two existentials because they are still AppState-held architectural collaborators, even if implementation selection happens in `init`.
+
+Line count: confirmed `wc -l` is 954, so 1050 is a reasonable +10% clean ceiling.
+
+Stored-property parsing: the brace-depth approach works on current `AppState.swift`. Top-level declarations sit at depth 0; method locals and closure locals sit at depth 1+. Lines with both opens/closes, like `guard let self else { return }`, stay inside method/closure depth and are not counted. The primitive exclusions do not miscategorize current top-level slots. `settings = SettingsManager()` is missed because it is `var`, matching the plan’s stated non-goal. `postCompletionWarningTask: Task<Void, Never>?` is excluded, correctly, and is also `var`.
+
+Mirror: do not use it. `AppState.init()` constructs real capture/ASR selections from defaults [AppState.swift:133-148], creates real storage/pipelines/backend objects :158-202, wires `SetupCoordinator` :213-218, applies settings :220-230, schedules Tasks :238 and :409, and wires many live callbacks. It may not always crash or hang, but it absolutely pulls runtime infrastructure into a test that only needs source structure.
+
+Cross-module public-TODO guard: plan claim of zero offenders is wrong. Current proposed broad window flags real and false positives. Real offender: `WhisperKitBackend.makeDecodeOptions` has `TODO: Phase 2 — narrow... cross-module` immediately above a `public func` [WhisperKitBackend.swift:156-157]. False positives include `DictationActivityProviding` due “Narrow contract” [Transcript.swift:89-91], `SilenceDetector` due “three-phase” [SilenceDetector.swift:72-74], `AudioCaptureManager.startCapture` due “single-phase” [AudioCaptureManager.swift:226-227], `TelemetryService.trackLIDAbstained` due `narrow_margin` [TelemetryService.swift:418-419], and `ProgressCallback` due `phaseString` [ASRProtocol.swift:5-8]. Tighten the regex to actual confessional comments, probably requiring `TODO` plus one of `narrow|temporary|cross-module|phase`, rather than raw words in a ±3 window.
+
+Dependency graph: revise before shipping. `Package.swift` says `EnviousWisprASR` depends on Core and Audio [Package.swift:57-65], `EnviousWisprServices` depends only on Core plus vendors :48-55, and `EnviousWisprLLM` depends only on Core :67-70. The proposed graph omits ASR→Audio and adds unused/stale Services→Audio/ASR and LLM→PostProcessing. More importantly, the script loops over all `Sources/*/` except `EnviousWispr`; it will include executable service targets with no `allowed` entries. Baseline would fail on six imports from `EnviousWisprASRService` and `EnviousWisprAudioService` [Package.swift:86-105]. Add allowed entries for those service targets or explicitly skip executable service dirs.
+
+Test placement is fine. `SetupCoordinatorTests.swift` uses `@testable import EnviousWispr` [SetupCoordinatorTests.swift:6] because it constructs internal app-shell types. The new source-reading tests do not need any EnviousWispr import.
+
+Phase F reconciliation: the shipped diff removed two `let`s, added one `let setup`, and removed one `Task` var. Under Phase E’s current metric, post-F is 19. The Phase F plan’s “19 → 17” claim [issue-501 plan:17] used a different/looser “concrete property” concept and its ship-criteria grep expected 17 [issue-501 plan:263], but the live tree does not match that. Document the metric change explicitly so future reviewers do not think Phase F under-delivered.
+
+Completeness: I would not add TranscriptionPipeline or WhisperKitPipeline ceilings in Phase E. Architecture rules already warn pipeline can become the next junk drawer [architecture-rules.md:48-52], and the plan’s §10 follow-up is the right place once pipeline shape stabilizes.
+
+Council-skip is acceptable only after the above fixes. Pure tests and CI script have no runtime user surface, but a broken CI gate can block all PRs, so baseline pass, intentional-failure verification, shellcheck, and correct workflow placement are mandatory. Also note `.github/workflows/pr-check.yml` currently has only `build-check`, no `lint` job [pr-check.yml:11-12]; wire the step into the actual job or create the lint job deliberately.

Phase E's locked metric counts existentials as collaborators because they still represent architectural seams that AppState owns. +# Phase E — Architecture regression tests (#502)
+
+Parent epic: #319 (Hardening & Refactors). Bible §11. Depends on: Phase F (#501) — SHIPPED in PR #503; ceiling inputs measured against post-F state.
+
+## Preface — Lane + Live UAT declaration (PR #498 — MANDATORY)
+
+- **Declared lane:** Code (mixed_pr: true — also touches CI/workflow + Docs/dev-tooling)
+- **Phase 3 obligations (per lane):**
+  - Code: tests + codex-review + skip-note for live-uat (pure-test PR, no user-visible surface)
+  - CI/workflow: workflow-run on pr-check.yml syntax
+  - Docs/dev-tooling: shellcheck on `scripts/check-dependency-direction.sh` + codex-prose on plan + arch-rules edits
+- **Live UAT:** N — no user-visible surface; tests are the validation. `skip-note.txt` will state: "Phase E ships only architecture regression tests + a CI script. No code path that runs at runtime in the shipped app changed. Tests passing IS the validation."
+
+## Preface — User Rubric
+
+User Rubric: N/A — Hardening & Refactors is internal-only (Bible §0.7). No user-facing surface.
+
+## 0. TL;DR
+
+Three new architecture-regression tests in `Tests/EnviousWisprTests/Architecture/` lock the post-Phase-F state of AppState so it does not silently re-accrete: a concrete-property-count ceiling (≤ 19), a line-count ceiling (≤ 1050 = post-F 954 + 10%), and a cross-module public-TODO grep guard that fails when a non-App module declares `public` with a confessional `TODO` comment containing one of "narrow", "temporary", "Phase N", or "cross-module" within ±3 lines. Re-introduces `scripts/check-dependency-direction.sh` (deleted with the brain system) and wires it into `.github/workflows/pr-check.yml` as a new `lint` job (none exists today) to enforce dep-direction at PR time. Narrows `WhisperKitBackend.makeDecodeOptions` from `public` → `package` (the existing TODO offender — fixable now that Swift 6 `package` access lets Pipeline call into ASR without app-public exposure). Documents the ceilings + cross-module grep pattern + dep-direction rules in `.claude/rules/architecture-rules.md`. Tier: SMALL. Est. LOC delta: ~250 (test code + bash + workflow YAML + 1-line ASR access change + docs).
+
+**Revised 2026-04-30 post-grounded-review:** Codex (`docs/audits/2026-04-30-phase-e-grounded-review.txt`) returned PROCEED-WITH-REVISIONS with four fixable issues: (1) cross-module-TODO regex was too broad — 5 false positives in current code (DictationActivityProviding, SilenceDetector, AudioCaptureManager, TelemetryService, ProgressCallback) plus 1 real offender (`WhisperKitBackend.makeDecodeOptions:156-157`); tightened to require `TODO` AND a structural keyword. (2) Dep-graph in §3.3 mismatched `Package.swift`; rebuilt against actual deps including the two XPC service executables. (3) `pr-check.yml` has no `lint` job today; create one deliberately. (4) Phase F's plan predicted post-F count of 17 but live is 19 because Phase F used a looser metric; Bible changelog notes the metric tightening. Real WhisperKitBackend offender is fixed in scope by narrowing `public func` → `package func` (1-line access change; no behavior change).
+
+## 1. Problem
+
+Phases A/B/C/D/F shaved AppState from a god-object trajectory toward a small set of cohesive collaborators. Without enforcement, the next session that adds "just one more service to AppState for convenience" recreates the trajectory. Bible §11 names this the fitness-function gap. The brain-system-era `scripts/check-dependency-direction.sh` was deleted when that system retired; the current `.git/hooks/pre-commit` is a no-op stub. SPM's implicit cyclic-import compile failure catches the worst case, but does not catch slow drift like "Audio module starts importing UI types via a typealias chain." Phase E re-introduces the lost enforcement and adds three architectural fitness tests calibrated to post-F state.
+
+## 2. Goals & non-goals
+
+### 2.1 Goals
+
+- Three regression tests in `Tests/EnviousWisprTests/Architecture/AppStateCeilingsTests.swift` and `Tests/EnviousWisprTests/Architecture/CrossModulePublicGuardTests.swift`.
+- Ceilings calibrated to post-Phase-F measurement (taken from worktree at HEAD of `feat/issue-502-phase-e-arch-tests`):
+  - AppState concrete-collaborator count ≤ 19 (counts top-level `let` declarations of types that are not stdlib/Foundation primitives, including existentials like `any AudioCaptureInterface`).
+  - AppState file line count ≤ 1050 (954 measured + 10% rounded down to a clean number).
+- Cross-module `public` TODO guard: any line in `Sources/EnviousWispr*/` (excluding `Sources/EnviousWispr/`, the App target, AND excluding the two XPC service executables `EnviousWisprAudioService` + `EnviousWisprASRService`) that declares `public` AND has a comment within ±3 lines containing both `TODO` AND one of [`narrow`, `temporary`, `cross-module`, or `phase\s*[a-z\d]+`] fails the test. The "TODO + structural-keyword" conjunction avoids the 5 false positives Codex grounded review identified (function names like `phaseString`, comment words like `narrow_margin` or "single-phase" used in their literal sense).
+- Narrow the existing real offender at `Sources/EnviousWisprASR/WhisperKitBackend.swift:155-157` from `public func makeDecodeOptions` → `package func makeDecodeOptions` and remove the confessional `TODO: Phase 2 — narrow ...` comment. Pipeline is in the same SPM package so `package` access is sufficient. This is a 1-line access modifier change + 2 lines of comment cleanup; no behavior change.
+- `scripts/check-dependency-direction.sh` re-introduced. Greps `import` statements per module, validates against an authoritative dep-graph encoded inline in the script, fails on backward edges (Pipeline importing App, Audio importing Pipeline, etc.). Wired into `.github/workflows/pr-check.yml` as a new step in the existing `lint` job.
+- Ceilings + cross-module rule + dep-direction graph documented in `.claude/rules/architecture-rules.md` under a new "Architectural Ceilings (enforced by tests)" section so future sessions discover the rule before tripping the test.
+- Audit meta-rec #1 (CI guard on cross-module public exposure) marked RESOLVED in Bible §11 changelog.
+
+### 2.2 Non-goals
+
+- No mutation of AppState or any Sources/. Phase E adds tests + a script + workflow + docs.
+- No reflection-based property counting. Stored-property detection runs against `AppState.swift` source text. Reasoning: AppState init has heavy side effects (audio capture, ASR manager, pipelines). Constructing a real instance in a test is fragile and pulls the heart path into a test that should only need the source file.
+- No coverage of `var` stored properties. Plain `var` and `lazy var` slots are mostly UI-affordance state (`isRecordingLocked`, `pendingNavigationSection`, `pendingPassiveChip`) or ObservationIgnored handler holders; they do not represent architectural collaborators in the Phase F sense. Future tightening can extend the test if needed.
+- No moving the dep-direction script's source-of-truth graph to a YAML/JSON file. Inline in bash for first cut. Phase E ships enforcement; future work can refactor the encoding.
+- No replacement for the no-op `.git/hooks/pre-commit` stub. CI is the enforcement layer; pre-commit hook stub stays as historical no-op for now.
+
+## 3. Design
+
+### 3.1 AppStateCeilingsTests.swift
+
+Two `@Test` cases. Both read `Sources/EnviousWispr/App/AppState.swift` from disk (path resolved relative to package root, since SwiftPM tests run with cwd = package root).
+
+```swift
+import Foundation
+import Testing
+
+@Suite struct AppStateCeilingsTests {
+
+  /// Concrete collaborator count ceiling. Locked at post-Phase-F baseline = 19.
+  /// Counts top-level `let` declarations on AppState whose type is non-primitive
+  /// (excludes Bool, Int, String, Optional<closure>, Task<...>, and other plain
+  /// values). Existentials (`any X`) count as collaborators.
+  ///
+  /// Increasing this ceiling is allowed but requires a Bible changelog entry
+  /// justifying the new collaborator. Run `swift test` to verify post-bump.
+  @Test func appStateConcreteCollaboratorCeilingHolds() throws {
+    let body = try classBodyOfAppState()
+    let count = countTopLevelLetCollaborators(in: body)
+    #expect(count <= 19, "AppState concrete-collaborator ceiling exceeded: \(count) > 19. See .claude/rules/architecture-rules.md `Architectural Ceilings`.")
+  }
+
+  /// Line-count ceiling. Locked at post-Phase-F (954 lines) + 10% rounded
+  /// to 1050. Soft backstop against scope creep.
+  @Test func appStateLineCountCeilingHolds() throws {
+    let url = appStateURL()
+    let source = try String(contentsOf: url, encoding: .utf8)
+    let lineCount = source.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false).count
+    #expect(lineCount <= 1050, "AppState line count exceeded: \(lineCount) > 1050. See .claude/rules/architecture-rules.md `Architectural Ceilings`.")
+  }
+}
+
+private func appStateURL() -> URL {
+  URL(fileURLWithPath: "Sources/EnviousWispr/App/AppState.swift")
+}
+
+private func classBodyOfAppState() throws -> String {
+  let source = try String(contentsOf: appStateURL(), encoding: .utf8)
+  guard let openRange = source.range(of: "final class AppState {") else {
+    throw POSIXError(.ENOENT)
+  }
+  let openIdx = source.index(before: openRange.upperBound)  // points at '{'
+  var depth = 0
+  var idx = openIdx
+  while idx < source.endIndex {
+    let c = source[idx]
+    if c == "{" { depth += 1 }
+    if c == "}" {
+      depth -= 1
+      if depth == 0 { return String(source[source.index(after: openIdx)..<idx]) }
+    }
+    idx = source.index(after: idx)
+  }
+  throw POSIXError(.EILSEQ)
+}
+
+private func countTopLevelLetCollaborators(in body: String) -> Int {
+  // Top-level = brace-depth 0 within class body. Match `let <ident>(:|\s*=)`
+  // (concrete or existential let). Skip primitives.
+  var depth = 0
+  var collaborators = 0
+  for line in body.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false) {
+    let opens = line.filter { $0 == "{" }.count
+    let closes = line.filter { $0 == "}" }.count
+    let depthForThisLine = depth - max(0, closes - opens)
+    if depthForThisLine == 0 {
+      let trimmed = line.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces)
+      let isLet = trimmed.hasPrefix("let ") || trimmed.hasPrefix("private let ")
+        || trimmed.hasPrefix("internal let ")
+      if isLet && !isPrimitiveTyped(trimmed) {
+        collaborators += 1
+      }
+    }
+    depth += opens - closes
+  }
+  return collaborators
+}
+
+private func isPrimitiveTyped(_ line: String) -> Bool {
+  let primitives = [": Bool", ": Int", ": String", ": Double", ": Float",
+                    "Task<", ": ((", "= false", "= true"]
+  return primitives.contains { line.contains($0) }
+}
+```
+
+The line/brace-depth approximation is intentional: AppState's class body uses standard formatting (one declaration per line, no inline closures at top scope after Phase A). If a future declaration spans multiple lines or includes a top-level closure literal, the test will need refinement; this is documented in the rules file.
+
+### 3.2 CrossModulePublicGuardTests.swift
+
+```swift
+import Foundation
+import Testing
+
+@Suite struct CrossModulePublicGuardTests {
+
+  /// Audit meta-rec #1: confessional `public` exposure across module boundaries
+  /// is a known architecture smell. This test fails if a `public` declaration
+  /// in any non-App module has a confessional-TODO comment within ±3 lines.
+  ///
+  /// Patterns flagged in the surrounding window: "narrow", "temporary",
+  /// "phase <X>", "cross-module", "TODO". Adjust the regex if a legitimate use
+  /// of one of these words triggers a false positive — but justify in the
+  /// Bible §11 changelog.
+  @Test func noConfessionalCrossModulePublicExists() throws {
+    let sourcesRoot = URL(fileURLWithPath: "Sources")
+    var offenders: [String] = []
+
+    // Exclude the executable targets: app shell + XPC services. These are not
+    // libraries that other modules consume, so cross-module-public is not a
+    // meaningful concept for them.
+    let executableTargets: Set<String> = [
+      "EnviousWispr",
+      "EnviousWisprAudioService",
+      "EnviousWisprASRService",
+    ]
+    let modules = try FileManager.default.contentsOfDirectory(
+      at: sourcesRoot, includingPropertiesForKeys: nil
+    ).filter { (try? $0.resourceValues(forKeys: [.isDirectoryKey]).isDirectory) == true }
+      .filter { !executableTargets.contains($0.lastPathComponent) }
+
+    for module in modules {
+      let files = try filesRecursively(at: module).filter { $0.pathExtension == "swift" }
+      for file in files {
+        let source = try String(contentsOf: file, encoding: .utf8)
+        let lines = source.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false)
+          .map(String.init)
+        for (idx, line) in lines.enumerated() {
+          if line.contains("public ") {
+            let lo = max(0, idx - 3)
+            let hi = min(lines.count - 1, idx + 3)
+            let window = lines[lo...hi].joined(separator: " ").lowercased()
+            // Tightened pattern post-Codex grounded review: require TODO AND a
+            // structural-cross-module keyword. Avoids false positives like
+            // `phaseString`, `narrow_margin`, "single-phase" in non-architectural
+            // contexts.
+            let hasTodo = window.contains("todo")
+            let hasStructural = window.contains("narrow")
+              || window.contains("temporary")
+              || window.contains("cross-module") || window.contains("cross module")
+              || window.range(of: #"phase\s*[a-z\d]+"#, options: .regularExpression) != nil
+            if hasTodo && hasStructural {
+              offenders.append("\(file.path):\(idx + 1): \(line.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces))")
+            }
+          }
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    #expect(offenders.isEmpty, "Confessional cross-module public found:\n\(offenders.joined(separator: "\n"))")

exec

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2	# Validates SPM target dependency direction by grepping `import` statements per module.
     3	# Fails on backward edges. Run from package root.
     4	#
     5	# Authoritative dep graph (verified against Package.swift on 2026-04-30).
     6	# Edit `permitted_imports_for` below when Package.swift changes (and update the
     7	# Bible if the new edge represents an architectural decision):
     8	#   EnviousWispr           -> Core, Storage, PostProcessing, Audio, Services, ASR, LLM, Pipeline (executable, top of stack)
     9	#   EnviousWisprAudioService -> Core, Audio (XPC executable)
    10	#   EnviousWisprASRService -> Core, ASR, Audio (XPC executable)
    11	#   EnviousWisprPipeline   -> Core, ASR, Audio, LLM, PostProcessing, Services, Storage
    12	#   EnviousWisprASR        -> Core, Audio
    13	#   EnviousWisprServices   -> Core
    14	#   EnviousWisprLLM        -> Core
    15	#   EnviousWisprAudio      -> Core
    16	#   EnviousWisprPostProcessing -> Core
    17	#   EnviousWisprStorage    -> Core
    18	#   EnviousWisprCore       -> (no app deps)
    19	#
    20	# Bash-3.2 compatible (macOS system /bin/bash). No associative arrays.
    21	
    22	set -euo pipefail
    23	
    24	# Returns the space-separated list of allowed EnviousWispr* deps for a target,
    25	# echoing nothing for "no deps allowed", and returning non-zero for unknown.
    26	permitted_imports_for() {
    27	  case "$1" in
    28	    EnviousWisprCore)              echo "" ;;
    29	    EnviousWisprAudio)             echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
    30	    EnviousWisprASR)               echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprAudio" ;;
    31	    EnviousWisprPostProcessing)    echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
    32	    EnviousWisprStorage)           echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
    33	    EnviousWisprLLM)               echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
    34	    EnviousWisprServices)          echo "EnviousWisprCore" ;;
    35	    EnviousWisprPipeline)          echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprASR EnviousWisprAudio EnviousWisprLLM EnviousWisprPostProcessing EnviousWisprServices EnviousWisprStorage" ;;
    36	    EnviousWisprAudioService)      echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprAudio" ;;
    37	    EnviousWisprASRService)        echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprASR EnviousWisprAudio" ;;
    38	    EnviousWispr)                  echo "EnviousWisprCore EnviousWisprStorage EnviousWisprPostProcessing EnviousWisprAudio EnviousWisprServices EnviousWisprASR EnviousWisprLLM EnviousWisprPipeline" ;;
    39	    *)                             return 1 ;;
    40	  esac
    41	}
    42	
    43	violations=0
    44	modules_scanned=0
    45	
    46	# Match `import EnviousWispr...` with:
    47	#   - Optional Swift attributes (e.g. `@preconcurrency`, `@_implementationOnly`,
    48	#     `@_spi(Internal)` — parenthesized argument allowed)
    49	#   - Optional leading whitespace
    50	#   - Optional import-kind tokens (`struct`, `class`, `enum`, `protocol`, `func`,
    51	#     `var`, `let`, `typealias`) for scoped imports like
    52	#     `import struct EnviousWisprPipeline.Foo`
    53	# Requires start-of-line anchoring to avoid matching literal text inside
    54	# comments or strings.
    55	import_kinds='(typealias|struct|class|enum|protocol|let|var|func)'
    56	import_attr='(@[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*(\([^)]*\))?[[:space:]]+)*'
    57	import_grep_pattern="^[[:space:]]*${import_attr}import[[:space:]]+(${import_kinds}[[:space:]]+)?EnviousWispr"
    58	
    59	for module_dir in Sources/*/; do
    60	  module=$(basename "$module_dir")
    61	  if ! permitted=$(permitted_imports_for "$module"); then
    62	    echo "DEP-DIRECTION: unknown target '$module' under Sources/ — add to permitted_imports_for() or remove" >&2
    63	    violations=$((violations + 1))
    64	    continue
    65	  fi
    66	  modules_scanned=$((modules_scanned + 1))
    67	  while IFS= read -r line; do
    68	    file=$(echo "$line" | cut -d: -f1)
    69	    # Strip the leading `path:lineno:` prefix from grep + any line/block comment
    70	    # tail before extracting the module. Stripping comments matters because an
    71	    # inline `// EnviousWisprCore` after a forbidden `import EnviousWisprPipeline`
    72	    # would otherwise be picked up by the greedy sed below.
    73	    code=$(echo "$line" | cut -d: -f3- | sed -E 's|//.*$||; s|/\*.*$||')
    74	    # Extract the imported module name. Handles plain (`import EnviousWisprX`)
    75	    # and scoped (`import struct EnviousWisprX.Foo`) forms by anchoring the
    76	    # capture to the first `EnviousWispr<rest>` token AFTER the `import` keyword.
    77	    # `${import_kinds}` already wraps the alternation in `(...)`, so the outer
    78	    # `(${import_kinds}[[:space:]]+)?` is group 1 and the inner alternation is
    79	    # group 2. The EnviousWispr capture is group 3.
    80	    imp=$(echo "$code" | sed -E "s/^.*import[[:space:]]+(${import_kinds}[[:space:]]+)?(EnviousWispr[A-Za-z_]*).*/\\3/")
    81	    case "$imp" in
    82	      EnviousWispr*)
    83	        if ! echo " $permitted " | grep -q " $imp "; then
    84	          echo "DEP-DIRECTION: $file: '$module' imports '$imp' (not in allowed: $permitted)"
    85	          violations=$((violations + 1))
    86	        fi
    87	        ;;
    88	    esac
    89	  done < <(grep -rEn "$import_grep_pattern" "$module_dir" || true)
    90	done
    91	
    92	if [ "$violations" -gt 0 ]; then
    93	  echo "FAIL: $violations dep-direction violation(s)" >&2
    94	  exit 1
    95	fi
    96	echo "OK: dep-direction clean across $modules_scanned modules"

--- AppState tests ---
     1	import Foundation
     2	import Testing
     3	
     4	/// Architecture regression tests for AppState.
     5	///
     6	/// Locks post-Phase-F (#501) state so AppState does not silently re-accrete
     7	/// toward a god-object. Tests parse the source file directly rather than
     8	/// constructing an AppState instance — AppState's init pulls in real audio
     9	/// capture, ASR, pipelines, and Tasks that should not run inside a unit test.
    10	///
    11	/// Ceilings are documented in `.claude/rules/architecture-rules.md` under
    12	/// `Architectural Ceilings`. Raising a ceiling requires a Bible changelog entry.
    13	@Suite struct AppStateCeilingsTests {
    14	
    15	  /// Concrete-collaborator count ceiling. Locked at post-Phase-F baseline = 19.
    16	  /// Counts top-level `let` declarations on AppState whose type is non-primitive.
    17	  /// Existentials (`any X`) count as collaborators.
    18	  @Test func appStateConcreteCollaboratorCeilingHolds() throws {
    19	    let body = try classBodyOfAppState()
    20	    let count = countTopLevelLetCollaborators(in: body)
    21	    #expect(
    22	      count <= 19,
    23	      """
    24	      AppState concrete-collaborator ceiling exceeded: \(count) > 19. \
    25	      See .claude/rules/architecture-rules.md `Architectural Ceilings`.
    26	      """)
    27	  }
    28	
    29	  /// File line-count ceiling. Locked at post-Phase-F (954) + ~10% rounded to 1050.
    30	  /// Soft backstop against scope creep.
    31	  @Test func appStateLineCountCeilingHolds() throws {
    32	    let url = appStateURL()
    33	    let source = try String(contentsOf: url, encoding: .utf8)
    34	    let lineCount = source.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false).count
    35	    #expect(
    36	      lineCount <= 1050,
    37	      """
    38	      AppState line count exceeded: \(lineCount) > 1050. \
    39	      See .claude/rules/architecture-rules.md `Architectural Ceilings`.
    40	      """)
    41	  }
    42	}
    43	
    44	private func appStateURL() -> URL {
    45	  // SPM tests run with cwd = package root.
    46	  URL(fileURLWithPath: "Sources/EnviousWispr/App/AppState.swift")
    47	}
    48	
    49	private func classBodyOfAppState() throws -> String {
    50	  let source = try String(contentsOf: appStateURL(), encoding: .utf8)
    51	  guard let openRange = source.range(of: "final class AppState {") else {
    52	    Issue.record("AppState declaration not found at expected path/shape")
    53	    throw POSIXError(.ENOENT)
    54	  }
    55	  let openIdx = source.index(before: openRange.upperBound)  // points at '{'
    56	  var depth = 0
    57	  var idx = openIdx
    58	  while idx < source.endIndex {
    59	    let c = source[idx]
    60	    if c == "{" { depth += 1 }
    61	    if c == "}" {
    62	      depth -= 1
    63	      if depth == 0 { return String(source[source.index(after: openIdx)..<idx]) }
    64	    }
    65	    idx = source.index(after: idx)
    66	  }
    67	  Issue.record("AppState class body has unbalanced braces")
    68	  throw POSIXError(.EILSEQ)
    69	}
    70	
    71	private func countTopLevelLetCollaborators(in body: String) -> Int {
    72	  // Top-level = brace-depth 0 within the class body.
    73	  // Match `let <ident>` declarations preceded by any combination of:
    74	  //   - Swift attributes (e.g. `@ObservationIgnored`, `@Published`)
    75	  //   - One access modifier (public/internal/private/fileprivate/package/open)
    76	  // Skip primitives (Bool/Int/String/closures/Tasks).
    77	  var depth = 0
    78	  var collaborators = 0
    79	  for line in body.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false) {
    80	    let opens = line.filter { $0 == "{" }.count
    81	    let closes = line.filter { $0 == "}" }.count
    82	    let depthForThisLine = depth - max(0, closes - opens)
    83	    if depthForThisLine == 0 {
    84	      let s = String(line)
    85	      if isCollaboratorLetDeclaration(s) && !isPrimitiveTyped(s) {
    86	        collaborators += 1
    87	      }
    88	    }
    89	    depth += opens - closes
    90	  }
    91	  return collaborators
    92	}
    93	
    94	private let collaboratorLetPattern: String = {
    95	  let attrs = #"(@[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*[[:space:]]+)*"#
    96	  let access = #"(public|internal|private|fileprivate|package|open)?"#
    97	  return "^[[:space:]]*\(attrs)\(access)[[:space:]]*let[[:space:]]+[A-Za-z_]"
    98	}()
    99	
   100	private func isCollaboratorLetDeclaration(_ line: String) -> Bool {
   101	  return line.range(of: collaboratorLetPattern, options: .regularExpression) != nil
   102	}
   103	
   104	private func isPrimitiveTyped(_ line: String) -> Bool {
   105	  // Architectural collaborators are concrete app/library types and protocol
   106	  // existentials. Plain values are not collaborators.
   107	  let primitives = [
   108	    ": Bool", ": Int", ": String", ": Double", ": Float",
   109	    "Task<", ": ((", "= false", "= true",
   110	  ]
   111	  return primitives.contains { line.contains($0) }
   112	}

--- public guard ---
     1	import Foundation
     2	import Testing
     3	
     4	/// Audit meta-rec #1 (Bible §11): confessional `public` exposure across module
     5	/// boundaries is a known architecture smell. This test fails if a `public`
     6	/// declaration in any non-executable module has a confessional `TODO` comment
     7	/// within ±3 lines.
     8	///
     9	/// Pattern requires both `TODO` AND a structural-cross-module keyword in the
    10	/// surrounding window. The conjunction avoids false positives like
    11	/// `phaseString` (function name), `narrow_margin` (telemetry field), and
    12	/// "single-phase" (literal phase counting in algorithms) that have no
    13	/// architectural meaning.
    14	@Suite struct CrossModulePublicGuardTests {
    15	
    16	  @Test func noConfessionalCrossModulePublicExists() throws {
    17	    let sourcesRoot = URL(fileURLWithPath: "Sources")
    18	    var offenders: [String] = []
    19	
    20	    // Exclude executable targets (app shell + XPC services). These are not
    21	    // libraries that other modules consume, so cross-module-public is not a
    22	    // meaningful concept for them.
    23	    let executableTargets: Set<String> = [
    24	      "EnviousWispr",
    25	      "EnviousWisprAudioService",
    26	      "EnviousWisprASRService",
    27	    ]
    28	
    29	    let modules = try FileManager.default.contentsOfDirectory(
    30	      at: sourcesRoot, includingPropertiesForKeys: nil
    31	    )
    32	    .filter { (try? $0.resourceValues(forKeys: [.isDirectoryKey]).isDirectory) == true }
    33	    .filter { !executableTargets.contains($0.lastPathComponent) }
    34	
    35	    for module in modules {
    36	      let files = try filesRecursively(at: module).filter { $0.pathExtension == "swift" }
    37	      for file in files {
    38	        let source = try String(contentsOf: file, encoding: .utf8)
    39	        let lines = source.split(separator: "\n", omittingEmptySubsequences: false)
    40	          .map(String.init)
    41	        for (idx, line) in lines.enumerated() where line.contains("public ") {
    42	          let lo = max(0, idx - 3)
    43	          let hi = min(lines.count - 1, idx + 3)
    44	          let window = lines[lo...hi].joined(separator: " ").lowercased()
    45	          let hasTodo = window.contains("todo")
    46	          let hasStructural =
    47	            window.contains("narrow")
    48	            || window.contains("temporary")
    49	            || window.contains("cross-module") || window.contains("cross module")
    50	            || window.range(of: #"phase\s*[a-z\d]+"#, options: .regularExpression) != nil
    51	          if hasTodo && hasStructural {
    52	            offenders.append(
    53	              "\(file.path):\(idx + 1): \(line.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces))")
    54	          }
    55	        }
    56	      }
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    #expect(
    60	      offenders.isEmpty,
    61	      """
    62	      Confessional cross-module `public` found (TODO + structural keyword within ±3 lines):
    63	      \(offenders.joined(separator: "\n"))
    64	      """)
    65	  }
    66	}
    67	
    68	private func filesRecursively(at dir: URL) throws -> [URL] {
    69	  guard
    70	    let enumerator = FileManager.default.enumerator(
    71	      at: dir, includingPropertiesForKeys: [.isRegularFileKey])
    72	  else { return [] }
    73	  return enumerator.compactMap { $0 as? URL }
    74	    .filter { (try? $0.resourceValues(forKeys: [.isRegularFileKey]).isRegularFile) == true }
    75	}

 succeeded in 0ms:
#!/usr/bin/env bash
# swift-test.sh — Run Swift Testing on CLT-only (no Xcode)
#
# This project builds with Command Line Tools only. Xcode is not installed.
# Paths are hardcoded to CLT locations. If running on a machine with Xcode,
# replace /Library/Developer/CommandLineTools with $(xcode-select -p).
#
# macOS CLT does not add Testing.framework or lib_TestingInterop.dylib
# to the default search paths. Five flags are needed:
#   1. -Xswiftc -F  (compile-time framework search)
#   2. -Xlinker -F  (link-time framework search)
#   3. -Xlinker -rpath for Frameworks dir (Testing.framework at runtime)
#   4. -Xlinker -rpath for usr/lib (Swift runtime libs)
#   5. -Xlinker -rpath for Developer/usr/lib (lib_TestingInterop.dylib)
#
# Usage:
#   scripts/swift-test.sh              # run all tests
#   scripts/swift-test.sh --filter Foo # filter to tests matching "Foo"
#   scripts/swift-test.sh --no-run     # compile tests only (used by release-preflight)

set -euo pipefail

CLT_BASE="/Library/Developer/CommandLineTools/Library/Developer"
FRAMEWORKS_DIR="${CLT_BASE}/Frameworks"
INTEROP_LIB_DIR="${CLT_BASE}/usr/lib"
USR_LIB_DIR="/Library/Developer/CommandLineTools/usr/lib"

if [ ! -d "$FRAMEWORKS_DIR/Testing.framework" ]; then
    echo "error: Testing.framework not found at $FRAMEWORKS_DIR" >&2
    echo "Requires macOS 26+ with Swift 6.3 Command Line Tools." >&2
    exit 1
fi

# Shared flag set — single source of truth for CLT Testing.framework wiring.
CLT_FLAGS=(
    -Xswiftc "-F${FRAMEWORKS_DIR}"
    -Xlinker "-F${FRAMEWORKS_DIR}"
    -Xlinker -rpath -Xlinker "${FRAMEWORKS_DIR}"
    -Xlinker -rpath -Xlinker "${USR_LIB_DIR}"
    -Xlinker -rpath -Xlinker "${INTEROP_LIB_DIR}"
)

NO_RUN=0
REMAINING_ARGS=()
for arg in "$@"; do
    case "$arg" in
        --no-run) NO_RUN=1 ;;
        *)        REMAINING_ARGS+=("$arg") ;;
    esac
done

if [[ $NO_RUN -eq 1 ]]; then
    exec swift build --build-tests "${CLT_FLAGS[@]}" "${REMAINING_ARGS[@]}"
fi

exec swift test "${CLT_FLAGS[@]}" "${REMAINING_ARGS[@]}"

exec
